4.2.1.2 Implementation Mechanisms and Procedures
46. To implement the abovementioned relevant laws and regulations for environmental protection
EIA and environmental pollution prevention & control, China, Hainan Province and the two Program
Counties have established and are gradually improving the relevant implementation mechanism,
which are listed in Error! Reference source not found..
                     Table 4-2 Mechanisms & Procedures for Environmental Pollution Control
 Implementation                                                   Description
 Mechanisms or
   Procedures
 1. Comprehensive Prevention and Control of Environmental Pollution
 Eco-            It is a new environmental management mechanism at the high-quality development stage established
 environment     and implemented based on differentiated and precise regional control, aiming at securing ecological
 zoning control  functions and improving environmental quality. The mechanism is fully integrated with terrestrial spatial
 is implemented planning and land use control. Terrestrial spaces of an administrative region are classified into urban,
 through the     agricultural and ecological spaces on the basis of the management zoning of various environmental
 establishment   elements (i.e. as air, water, soil, ecology, sound, and marine) to determine eco-environment control units
 of an eco-      (zones). These units are delineated based on factors such as eco-environment quality and resource
 environment     utilization status. Hainan Province, including the island and its adjacent waters, have been classified into
 access list.    three types of eco-environmental control units from the perspective of ecological and environmental
                 protection, namely priority protection units, key control units and general control units, so as to achieve
                 differentiated control and carry out regular adjustments and dynamic updates in a coordinated manner.
                 Implementing eco-environment zoning control has provided rigid constraints for the implementation of
                 strategic and planning environmental impact assessments, as well as the approval of EIA for construction
                 projects. It has also provided spatial control for other environmental management assignments. Through
                 eco-environment zoning control, the requirements for pollution prevention and control are advanced to the


                                                             23
Implementation                                                     Description
Mechanisms or
  Procedures
                 spatial planning level, achieving the effect of source prevention and spatial constraints; based on the
                 environmental carrying capacity of different zones, a differentiated list of ecological and environment access
                 list is precisely compiled, and requirements for controlling pollutant emissions and preventing
                 environmental pollution risks are proposed.
Environmental    To implement the EIA system, China has established a detailed and comprehensive catalogue for
impact           screening environmental impacts and classifying EIA processes proportional to project nature, location,
screening and    scale, environmental context, and so on. Environmental impacts of construction projects are classified into
classification   three levels: Class A – High and substantial impacts; Class B - small to moderate impacts; and Class C -
                 minor impacts. Correspondingly, the EIA instruments are divided into three categories: EIA report (Class
                 A), EIA form (Class B), and EIA registration (Class C). The Technical Guidelines for EIA has specific sub-
                 guidelines specifically targeting key polluting industries/sectors
                 Pollution management activities to be supported under RA2 of the Project are subject to EIA-Form
                 preparation or EIA registration without the need for EIA-report preparation. This section only gives
                 an initial analysis of EIA classification related to the Project activities and specific types of EIA
                 instruments applicable to each construction activity will be determined by local BEEs during the Project
                 implementation.
EIA Follow-up           Environmental ‘Three Simultaneousness’. Design, construction, and operation of a pollution control
and              facility that is to support a construction project must be carried out simultaneously with the main parts. The
supervision      Project design report must include a specific chapter to specify mitigation measures, pollution control
                 facilities, and necessary cost estimates. To ensure the pollution control facilities are built properly as
                 designed, the PIU is responsible for including the physical works of pollution control facilities into civil works
                 contracts and ensuring construction or installing schedule and budget to be sufficient. The PIU is also
                 responsible for implementing other mitigation measures that are recommended in the EIA instruments and
                 approval documents. The Project is not allowed to start operation until all pollution control facilities and
                 mitigation measures have passed the environmental acceptance check for construction completion.
                        Environmental management during construction. PIUs (county-level WRBs, ARABs, etc.) are
                 responsible for implementing proper measures to mitigate environmental impacts during construction. As
                 per China’s ‘Standard Construction Bidding Regulations’, a bidding document should include an
                 environmental protection chapter to include the mitigation measures. A standard civil work contract will also
                 include an environmental protection chapter to clarify the contractor’s duties on environmental management
                 such as implementing mitigation measures. After the contract is signed, the contractor should develop
                 construction implementation programs which should include environmental management schemes that are
                 reviewed and agreed upon by the PIU and supervision engineers before construction commissioning.
                 During construction, the PIU and supervision engineers will oversee the implementation of the
                 environmental management plans. EEBs conduct routine regulatory by checking pollution control measures
                 taken against mitigation measures proposed in EIA.
                        Environmental acceptance checks for construction completion. When construction of a project is
                 completed, the PIU (or with the assistance of qualified agencies) should carry out a specific check f or
                 environmental acceptance, in accordance with Technical Guidelines for Environmental Protection
                 Acceptance of Construction Projects - Pollution Impacts. PIU should prepare, disclose its Environmental
                 Acceptance Check Report, and seek relevant experts’ comments. The PIU should disclose the
                 environmental acceptance check report within five working days once the report is completed and keep it
                 open to the public for at least 20 working days. Within five working days after the disclosure, the PIU should
                 log into the national platform for environmental acceptance check to upload the Project description, the
                 review comments on the environmental acceptance check, and other basic information. This information
                 will be disclosed to the public by BEEs that will supervise the procedures of the environmental acceptance
                 check, register the relevant information for filing. When environmental acceptance check is deemed
                 acceptable, the PIU shall apply for or renew its pollution discharge permit.
                        EIA Follow-up supervision. The EIA follow-up supervision is to check whether BEEs have justly
                 fulfilled their duties in EIA approval, whether technical review agencies have provided rational review
                 comments on EIA, whether EIA agencies have done accurate EIA based on true data and in a reliable way,
                 and whether PIUs have gone through proper EIA procedures and conducting public consultation as
                 required. The follow-up supervision after EIA is to check whether BEEs have fulfilled their duties in ‘Three
                 Simultaneousness’ supervision and whether PIUs have implemented the ‘Three Simultaneousness’ and
                 other environmental management measures as required in the stages of design, construction,
                 environmental acceptance check, and operation.
Classified       As per Pollution Discharge Permit Management Measures, pollution discharge permit refers to an
management of    administrative license that manages the discharge of pollutants from the fixed pollution sources of
pollutant        enterprises and other production and business operators. In 2016, the State Council issued the
discharge        Implementation Plan for Controlling Pollutant discharge by means of Permit System. By 2020, all fixed
permits          pollution sources across China, including Hainan Province have completed the issuance of pollutant
                 discharge permits covering all such sources. The Ministry of Ecology and Environment (MEE) is
                 implementing full-process management and multi-pollutants comprehensive control for fixed pollution
                 sources, achieving systematic, scientific, legal, refined, and information-based "one-permit" management.
                 The pollutants discharge permit, as a carrier, clearly records the types, concentrations, emissions, emission
                 methods and environmental management requirements of the pollutants of the polluting units, serving as
                 the sole certificate for legal pollutants discharge. Based on the amount of pollutant emissions and the extent
                 of environmental impact, the polluting units are classified into three categories: focused management (with
                 large amounts of pollutant generation, emissions or significant environmental impact), simplified

      3. Agricultural NPS pollution management
 Approaches on BRARs at all levels issued guidelines on scientific fertilization of major crops and set up teams of fertilizer
 nutrient            experts to provide technical guidance on managing nutrients and reduced use of fertilizer with improved
 management          efficiency. Main approaches includes (a) advancing test-based fertilization with formula constantly
 and reduced         improved; (b) planting green manures to promote energy saving an low-carbon agricultural development;
 use of              (c) replacing chemical fertilizer with organic fertilizer or mixture of the two; (d) promoting returning straw
 chemical            to the field to maximize the substitution and reduction of potassium fertilizer; (e) optimizing composition of
 fertilizers with    fertilizers by means of application of special formula fertilizers (for example, alkaline fertilizer [applicable
 improved            to Hunan where soil is dominated by acidic red soil], water-soluble fertilizer, and soil conditioner, selected
 efficiency          rationally according to soil, role, nutrient demand of crops, and local ecosystem); (f) improving fertilization
                     methods, such as fertigation, deeper mechanical fertilization, foliar fertilization, and so on; (g)
                     emphasizing provision of technical training, etc.
 Crops               The government supports service entities with appropriate crop protection expertise and equipment to
 protection and      carry out socialized, large-scale and intensive crop pest control services, and takes comprehensive
 reduced use of      measures such as agronomic, physical, biological and chemical measures to carry out pest control
 pesticides.         services to effectively ensure agri-food quality and eco-environmental safety.
                     Promotion of reduced use of pesticides with improved efficiency: measures adopted include: 1)
                     advanced application instruments suitable for local terrain to improve the adhesion rate, or the use of
                     drone plant protection operations to improve the utilization of pesticides; (2) The implementation of high-
                     efficiency and low-toxicity pesticides: the list of low-toxicity and low-residue pesticides recommended by
                     the Ministry of Agriculture and Rural Affairs (MARA); (3) Green control: including agricultural control (such
                     as tillage and other agronomic measures), physical and chemical control (such as insecticidal lamps, sex
                     attractants, insect nets, armyworm boards), biological control (such as aphids natural enemies ladybugs,
                     microorganisms and other biological pesticides), scientific drug technology (such as not exceeding the
                     scope of application of pesticides, the establishment of bug monitoring system); (4) Improve the
                     organizational model: such as unified defense rule, third-party professional services; (5) Pesticide
                     sources control: The county Agriculture and Rural Bureau (through the agricultural comprehensive law
                     enforcement brigade under its jurisdiction) supervises and inspects the license of pesticide operators,
                     pesticide quality and safety, and conducts training for pesticide users.
 Management of Although pesticide packaging waste is exempted from hazardous material management as per the
 pesticides          National Hazardous Waste List (2021 Edition) during collection, transportation, utilization and disposal
 package waste       processes, the construction of transfer stations is subject to EIA, which assesses the potential impact on
                     soil, groundwater and propose mitigation measures. After recycling, pesticide package waste must be
                     treated harmlessly.
 Crop straw          Hainan Province has implemented a province-wide ban on open-air burning of straw. In the two Program
 utilization and     counties, the following comprehensive utilization measures are being carried out: 1) Fertilization
 management          utilization: including directly shredding and returning paddy straw to the farmland when harvesting; and 2)
                     other crops straw are piled-up for composing or biologically reacted to produce organic fertilizers
 Agricultural        Main measures for agricultural mulch management include: 1) Reduced use of mulch by promoting rational
 mulch               application of mulch technology, strengthening rotation and intercropping system, demonstrating
 management          technologies of multi-purpose use of mulch and inter-row mulching; 2) Standardization of agricultural mulch
                     by strictly implementing the Polyethylene Blow-Molded Agricultural Mulch (GB13735-2017) standard and
                     promoting the application of thicker films (over 0.01mm), and moderately promoting the technology of
                     replacing with fully biodegradable films; 3) Mechanization of agricultural mulch collection by enhancing
                     research and development of mulching recovery machinery and the integration of related technologies; 4)
                     Specialized recycling of agricultural mulch supported by local governments to provide financial support to
                     socialized service organizations and enterprises engaged in the recycling and processing of agricultural
                     mulch, thereby establishing a recycling and processing system; 5) Provision of trainings on recycling of
                     agricultural mulch; 6) Establishing an annual ledger for the recovery of agricultural mulch, regularly
                     supervision the recycling of used agricultural mulch led of ARABs. If there are any serious problems of
                     pollution caused by used agricultural mulch, the event will be publicly exposed, and necessary
                     accountability measures will be taken.


4.2.1.3 Institutional Organization and Performance
47. DEE/EEBs: EIA is the legal guarantee for restricting the environmental access of projects and
plans, and it is the first defense line for protecting the green mountains and clear waters during
development. DEE/EEBs at all levels carry out regulate over environment pollution by implementing
mechanisms of eco-environment zoning control, EIA at front end and follow-up supervision by
implementing mechanisms of acceptance-check at construction completion, the environmental
“three simultaneousness”, pollution discharge permits, and environmental monitoring.

                                                                 26
⚫      Hainan Provincial DEE: under which there are such divisions as EIA & pollutants discharge
       management, marine environmental management, eco-environmental monitoring, soil &
       agricultural management, water environment management; and eco-environmental
       administrative law enforcement bureaus in place, technically supported by academy of eco-
       environmental science and technology and Provincial eco-environmental monitoring center
       stations. DEE is responsible for the formulation and dynamic update of the province-wide
       environmental protection access list, coordinating the management of pollutants discharge
       permits, organizing province-wide regular environment quality monitoring and management of
       pollution sources (including point sources and NPS) monitoring network, periodically disclose
       monitoring results of water environmental quality of rivers (including rivers flowing into marine),
       regulate fixed pollutants discharge outlets, where automatic on-line monitoring instruments are
       installed as per their pollutants discharge permit requirement and connected with environmental
       monitoring network managed by DEE. DEE also provide guidance and coordination to local
       EEBs in the province. Hainan province established a province-wide “Eco-environmental Zoning
       Control Application Management System” in 2021 for integrated management of data available
       at provincial and county levels. The said system enables DEE/EEBs at Provincial and county
       levels to manage the eco-environmental units/zones integrated. It integrates complex spatial
       elements and constraint indicators and clearly defines them in specific management units
       covering all sorts of eco-environmental units/zones in the Hainan Province. This system is an
       on-line, real-time information platform for regulatory of eco-environment zoning control. DEE
       cooperates with DWR, DARABs on promotion of urban and rural domestic pollution control,
       agricultural NPS control. In considering the characteristics of the coastal areas of Hainan and
       the requirements for marine ecological environment protection, particularly for management of
       pollution from land-based and marine-based aquaculture production, DEE proposed specific
       regulations such as the Environmental Protection Management Regulations for Land-based
       Aquaculture Projects in Hainan Province and the Aquaculture Effluent Discharge Standards
       (DB46/475-2023), which are local mandatory standards.
⚫      County-level EEBs of the two Program Counties: there are positions or sections of EIA and
       pollutants discharge management (1-4 staff), water environmental management or water & air
       environmental management (1-7 staff) in place. Since 2021, when the two counties
       implemented ecological environment zoning control, concurrently with Hainan Province, they
       have fully utilized the provincial "Ecological Environment Zoning Control Application
       Management System in the fields of resource development, industrial layout and structural
       adjustment, urban planning, project site selection, and review & approval of EIAs, thereby
       reducing the risks in the early decision-making of projects. With technical assistance of
       consultancy agencies, the two bureaus updated their county-level ecological environment
       zoning control and the ecological environment access list (2025) and submitted to DEE for
       filing/registration management. Their routine work includes organizing experts to conduct
       technical reviews of EIA documents before submitting them to the County Business Environment
       Construction Bureau for approval 7 . EEBs work together with the County Integrated Law
       Enforcement Bureau to conduct law enforcement inspection of affairs related to EIAs, pollutants
       discharge permit, and environmental pollution. For example, Changjiang County EEB has been
       making use of the existing monitoring network to conduct continuous and close monitoring of
       surface water and other water bodies and has been persistently promoting the remediation of
       pollutants discharge outlets flowing into marine. In 2024, the EEB updated its statistic ledger of
       pollutants discharge outlets flowing into marine and linked them into the national management
       system. Its yearly supervision monitoring work covers, among the others, 291 pollutants
       discharge outlets flowing into marine. In the first half of 2025, the EEB urged the county WRB,
       ARAB to further accelerate the remediation of discharge outlets flowing into rivers and marine.
       Lingshui County EEB in the past 3 years, reviewed 109 projects EIAs for approval, issued
       pollutants discharge permits for 42 entities, cooperated with WRB to conduct quarterly
       environmental monitoring on the effluent quality of urban WWTPs, conducted quarterly
       environmental monitoring on the tail water quality of aquaculture. According to the "Monthly

7 County Business Environment Construction Bureau: established in 2022 with the aim of optimizing the business environment through integrated institutional innovation and

promoting the construction of the Hainan Free Trade Port. It is mainly responsible for provision of optimized services and coordinated resources and does not directly participate
in technical approval processes. Each government line agencies assumes the core functions in the approval processes of their respective authorities.


                                                                                       27
           Report on Environmental Monitoring of Hainan Province" released by the Hainan Provincial
           Environmental Monitoring Center, the water quality of the coastal areas of Lingshui County in
           the spring and summer of 2024 was excellent. The proportion of water areas with excellent &
           good quality was 100%, belonging to Class I water quality, remaining the same as the previous
           year.
48. DWR/WRBs: are the government line authorities responsible for “integrated management of six
waters8”, including urban and rural domestic wastewater management, and river & riparian water.
Under the two Program Counties’ WRBs, there are sections of water resources (2 staff), urban &
rural water (4 staff) in place. These sections have following responsibilities related to the Project:
⚫          River/lakes eco-environment management: WRBs develop and implement Work Plan for the
           Comprehensive Implementation of River/Lake Chief System at the County Level, provide
           guidance on delineating of water bodies and their riparian and the management of them, provide
           guidance on the protection & rehabilitation of river/lake eco-environment and water connection
           among rivers & lakes; supervise the performance of each river/lake chief, and develop plans for
           river protection and utilization;
⚫          Urban and rural domestic wastewater management: WRBs take over WWTPs and their
           sewer networks constructed by the county Housing & Urban & Rural Construction Bureaus and
           develop plan for rural domestic wastewater management and under construction and
           management of urban and rural WWTPs/WWTFs and their sewer networks. Contract out the
           management of the operation and maintenance (O&M) of WWTPs/WWTFs and their sewer
           networks. Changjiang WRB contracted to two professional companies to manage the O&M of
           all urban WWTPs and their sewer networks, and O&M of all rural WWTFs and their sewer
           networks respectively. Lingshui County WRB contracted to one professional company to
           manage the O&M of both urban WWTPs and rural WWTFs and their sewer networks. O&M
           performance evaluation indicators were established, and quarterly evaluations were conducted.
           The O&M companies were paid based on the assessment scores to ensure the normal operation
           with treated effluent quality compliance with the applicable standards. For example, the
           evaluation of O&M performance of rural WWTFs and their sewer networks include 10 indicators:
           namely, working mechanism established for maintenance, staff assigned for operation and
           maintenance, phone numbers dedicated for reporting malfunctioning of mechanical equipment,
           repairing equipment, flow and quality if influent and effluent and social assessment.
⚫          To prevent secondary pollution to the environment resulting from surplus sludge, the sludge
           from small and medium-sized WWTPs and WWTFs are hauled by sealed tanker trucks to large-
           scale WWTPs (or the county seat WWTP) equipped with sludge dewatering machine for
           dewatering until the moisture content is below 80%, before being finally disposed of. Surplus
           sludge are disposed of: 1) incinerated together with domestic solid waste in waste-to-energy
           incineration plant，2）used by an enterprise to produce nutrient soil (mixed with crop straw,
           wool ships and kitchen waste) for producing biomass fuel that are used by biomass power plant;
           3) Co-processed in cement kiln (see Table 3-1). Throughout the entire process of sludge
           haulage and disposal, the O&M companies have signed sludge disposal contracts with the
           downstream companies receiving sludge. The contracts include a provision that the sludge shall
           not be used as raw material for agricultural organic fertilizers and shall not enter into the food
           chain. Triple bills were used for haulage of sludge, one bill was maintained by the O&M company,
           one bill was handed over to WRB, and one bill was used for random inspections by EEB.
⚫          Compliance with environmental protection procedures: as PIUs for river/lake eco-
           environmental rehabilitation activity, and urban & rural domestic waste water management
           activity, during projects preparation, WRBs contracted with EIA consultancy firm to carry EIAs
           in parallel with the feasibility studies and have EIAs reviewed and approved; When the Project
           was completed, environmental acceptance-check was conducted to implement the
           environmental "three simultaneous" mechanism. WRBs, or urge the contracted O&M Company,
           apply for pollutants discharge permit for WWTPs/WWTFs. As per requirements of the pollutants
           discharge permit, O&M company carry out, or entrust the third professional party to carry out

8 Integrated management of six waters” refer to treating wastewater, securing water supply, draining water-log, preventing floods, saving water use and improving sea water

quality.


                                                                                      28
       sampling and monitoring of water qualities of influent and effluent and surplus sludge of
       WWTPs/WWTFs and report the monitoring results on the national pollutant discharge permit
       information management platform. In addition, urban WWTPs are basically installed on-line
       monitoring instruments for influent and effluent quality, connected to the on-line regulatory
       network established by the MEE.
⚫      County WRBs or contracted O&M companies applied for pollutant discharge permits for their
       respected WWTPs or WWTFs. According to the requirements of the pollutant discharge permit,
       the O&M company entrusts professional environmental monitoring institutions to regularly
       monitor the water qualities of influents and effluents and sludge and report the results on the
       national pollutant discharge permit information management platform. In addition, most urban
       sewage treatment plants are equipped with online monitoring devices for influents and effluents,
       which are connected to the online monitoring network established by MEE.
49. DARA/ARABs: are responsible for providing sectoral guidance, service and management of
    agricultural NPS pollution, recycling and multi-purpose utilization of agricultural wastes (including
    straw, agricultural mulch, packaging waste, etc.).             Under the policy guidance of the
    Implementation Plan for the Control and Supervision of Agricultural Non-point Source Pollution
    (Trial) jointly issued by the MEE and MARA, local governments, DARA/ARABs and relevant local
    authorities at all levels optimize the spatial layout of agricultural production, formulate medium or
    long-term plans for controlling agricultural NPS pollution, assign specific tasks for prevention and
    reduction, and adopt differentiated measures for pollution control in different regions and sources.
    ARABs actively promote approaches of "source reduction & recycling - process interception -
    end treatment/disposal". Under the two Program counties’ ARABs, there are sections of farmland
    (1-2 staff), crops production (2 staff) in place, supported by modern agricultural development
    service centers (11-12 staff). They are responsible for management of agricultural NPS pollution
    prevention and control. Their specific assignment related to the Project include:
⚫      High standard farmland construction: the activities carried out to alleviate or eliminate the
       main restrictive factors for farming and comprehensively enhance the production capacity of
       farmland, including land leveling, irrigation and drainage, on-farm roads, farmland protection and
       ecological environment protection, farmland power transmission and distribution, as well as soil
       improvement, removal of obstacle soil layers, and soil fertility enhancement. Through the high
       standard farmland construction, farmlands are improved into high standard and ecological ones
       by applying systematic engineering measures and the application of ecological technologies.
       High standard farmland construction enhances not only agricultural production efficiency, but
       also achieves soil improvement, water-saving irrigation, and soil and water conservation. It will
       also help reduce fertilizers input, effectively intercept sediment and pollutant emission, control
       agricultural NPS pollution, and improve the surrounding water environment.
⚫      Reduced used of chemical fertilizers & pesticides with improved efficiency: In responding
       to the "dual reduction" tasks issued by the Provincial DARA, county-level ARABs formulated and
       implemented annual plans on reduced use of chemical fertilizers and pesticides with improved
       efficiency, or subsidy project implementation plans. They provide services and take actions on
       test-based soil fertilization, specialized services for integrated crop pests control 9 by
       establishing sampling & monitoring points on farmland for fertilizer and pesticide usage and soil
       fertility. For example, Changjiang-County ARAB established 20 sampling and monitoring points
       for testing the use of chemical fertilizers and pesticides, 9 sampling and monitoring points for
       soil fertility, its services on test-based soil fertilization cover a total farmland area of 23,334 ha,
       a large proportion of the county’s farmland. It also provides services on crop pest prevention
       and control. In Lingshui County, the use of chemical fertilizers in 2024 was reduced by more
       than 12.6%, compared to that of 2020. In the first half of 2025, unmanned aerial vehicles (UAV)
       were used to control over 1696 ha of paddy pests.
⚫       Recycling and multi-purpose utilization of crops straw: In responding to ARABs tasks
       issued by the Provincial DARA, county-level ARABs formulated annual work plan for recycling

9 specialized services for integrated crop pests control refers to the behaviours where specialized pest control service organizations provide pest and disease control services for

agricultural producers



                                                                                        29
    and multi-purpose utilization of crop straw. High altitude smoke monitoring and alarm points
    were established to implement mechanism of banning on open-air burning of straw. Township
    governments bare responsibility of banning on open-air burning of straw by establishing
    mechanism of “smallholders’ collection, village sorting, township transferring”. Smallholders are
    urged to collect straw promptly store straw at designated collection stations where the township
    organize teams to transfer vegetable and fruit stalks to waste-to-energy incinerators for disposal.
    In Lingshui County, rural revitalization project funds were used in 2022 to support an enterprise
    to have established and operated a plant where crops straw is mixed with livestock & poultry
    manure for processing into organic fertilizer. The County ARAB has considered the inclusive of
    constructing other similar plants in its plan for high standard farmland construction.
⚫   Recycling and multi-purpose utilization of other agricultural wastes: In responding to
    ARABs tasks issued by the Provincial DARA, county-level ARABs gradually improve its working
    mechanism on Recycling and multi-purpose utilization of other agricultural wastes by subsidizing
    sellers, small enterprises to construct facilities for recycling and multi-purpose utilization of other
    agricultural wastes (including agricultural mulch and straw). For example, Changjiang County
    has established a mechanism for the recycling of agricultural mulch which adopts the approach
    of "collection by marketing entities and disposal by specialized enterprises” and implemented
    mandatory waste recycling and centralized disposal. Each township has established temporary
    waste collection points for farmland waste to ensure timely collection and avoid secondary
    pollution. Through both online and offline channels, the ARAB carried out publicity activities for
    the recycling of agricultural mulch among farmers and extended basic knowledge about the
    recycling of agricultural mulch to the farmers. This aimed to enhance the villagers' awareness
    of not littering, not landfilling, and not open-air burning of agricultural waste. Those townships
    where agricultural mulch are largely used were selected as pilots to invite enterprises engaged
    in agricultural mulch recycling and to invest cycling facilities for processing collected mulch into
    reprocessed plastic pellets. The ARAB also provided guidance to township governments to,
    based on the planting situation of the farmland contracted by cooperatives or enterprises in their
    respective towns, sign warranties supported by deposit funds to ensure agricultural mulch are
    timely collected and transferred to the recycling points designated by township governments
    where the collected mulch is to be further hauled by the third party to plants for producing
    reprocessing plastic pellets. The county ARAB carried out pilot projects for application of
    biodegradable plastic mulch and promoted the use of thicker plastic mulch. To date, most
    agricultural goods supply stores in Changjiang County no longer sell agricultural mulch with
    thickness lower than 0.015 mm. Lingshui County ARAB, worked jointly with the county EEB to
    supervise the licensed operation of pesticide dealers. It also signs contracts with third-party
    professional agencies and regularly collects pesticide packaging waste from farmland and hauls
    them into waste-to-energy incinerators for harmless disposal. The existing points and multi-
    purpose utilization facilities of agricultural wastes are inadequate, serving only limited farmland
    areas, therefore these points and facilities are to be supported under the Project. The
    construction and operation of such collection points and processing facilities will be subject to
    EIA, environmental “three simultaneousness”, pollution discharge permits management, and
    subject to DEE/EEBs regulatory as discussed in this section.
4.2.1.4 Assessment
50. Hainan Province and the two Program counties have established and continuously improved
effective management mechanisms in the areas of environmental pollution prevention and control to
complain with national and local laws and regulations. These mechanisms have been proven
effective in the collection and treatment of urban and rural domestic sewage, the prevention and
control of agricultural non-point source pollution and have achieved remarkable results. The WB
team found through field visits and discussion with stakeholders that activities similar to typical ones
to be supported by the Project have been subjected to EIA and follow-up management. DEE/EEBs
at all levels collaborated with relevant government authorities to conduct front-end, follow-up
inspections and supervision in various forms, to avoid, prevent, reduce or mitigate the adverse
environmental impacts of the construction projects as much as possible. This environmental pollution
management system has proven to be basically compliance with the Bank’s core principles.
Nevertheless, gaps are found in managing rural domestic waste water due to the characteristics of
scattered, small-scale, and rich rainfalls in Hainan Province and inadequate participation of

                                                    30
beneficiary villagers: rural WWTFs sometimes have no effluent, face with challenge of overflows of
mixed rainwater and sewage during rainy days because of blockage of sewer networks, that are in
some cases, misconnected to the households, especially the newly built houses, lack of such
devices as oil separators, bars necessary for preventing sized solid waste from entering into the
system. These issues have affected the efficiency of collecting and treating rural domestic sewage.
Therefore, the ESSA recommend a PAP (see chapter 7).
4.2.2 Ecological Conservation Management Sub-system
4.2.2.1 Applicable Legal and Regulatory Framework
51. Similar to environmental pollution management system, based on the Environmental Protection
Law the People’s Republic of China (PRC) and Marine Environmental Protection Law of PRC, China
has established numerous laws and regulations related to the conservation of natural resource,
biodiversity and natural habitats. In June 2019, the General Office of the Central Committee of the
Communist Party of China and the General Office of the State Council issued the Guiding Opinions
on Establishing a Nature Reserve System with National Parks as the Main Body, which aims to
accelerate the establishment of a nature protected areas system with national parks as the main
body, provide high-quality ecological products, and promote the construction of a beautiful China.
Since 2014, China has been promoting a nationwide important institutional innovation for
environmental protection, namely establishing and implementing the ecological protection redlines
(ERLs) system. By 2023, Hainan Province has completed, like the rest of the country, its delineation
of ERLs. Important ecological functional areas, ecological environment sensitive areas, and
vulnerable areas have been delineated into the scope of the ERLs. In August 2022, the MNR, MEE
and National Forestry and Grassland Administration issued the "Notice on Strengthening the
Management of ERLs (Trial)", which required strengthening the control of human activities and
standardizing the approval procedures for activities occupying land, marine, and islands that triggers
the ERLs and strictly regulating the ERLs by following Land Management Law, Marine Area Use
Management Law, Environmental Protection Law, Environmental Impact Assessment Law, Water
Pollution Prevention and Control Law, Marine Environmental Protection Law, Forest Law, Grassland
Law, Wetland Protection Law, Natural Reserve Regulations, Scenic Area Regulations, Forest Law
Implementation Regulations, etc., plus Hainan local regulations formulated by Hainan Province in
accordance with these national laws and in light of the local actual conditions and characteristics.
These laws & regulations have provided a legal basis for the above-mentioned authorities to manage
the potential ecological impact/risks of the Project activities.

4.2.2.2 Implementation Mechanisms and Procedures
52. To effectively implement the aforementioned laws and regulations on natural ecological
protection, protection of nature reserves, and EIA, China, Hainan Province, and the two Program
counties have all established and are gradually improving the following implementation mechanisms
(see Table 4-5 below).
                          Table 4-4 Mechanisms & Procedures for Ecological Conservation
 Implementation                                                       Description
 Mechanisms or
   Procedures
 1．Natural Ecology Conservation
 ERLs       and     ERLs mechanism is the most stringent ecological conservation mechanism in China, essentially serving to
 limited human      safeguard the bottom line of ecological environment. DNRP/NRPBs, DEE/EEBs, FBs at all levels have jointly
 activities         delineated those important ecological functional areas into the ERLs, including areas with functions of water
 accessible to      conservation, maintaining biodiversity, soil and water conservation, windbreak and sand fixation, stability of
 the ERLs           coastal ecology, etc., as well as sensitive and fragile ecological areas such as areas prone to water and soil
                    erosion, land desertification, rocky desertification, and salinization. Since China launched the pilot program for
                    ERLs in 2013 until 2023, the delineation of ERLs throughout China has been fully completed.
                    According to the Regulations on the Management of Ecological Protection Red Lines in Hainan Province
                    (2022), Hainan Province has designated following areas into the scope of ERLs:1) the natural protected areas
                    (covering national parks, nature reserves, and natural parks (after being adjusted and optimized), 2) mangrove
                    wetlands outside protected areas, 3) drinking water source protection areas outside protected areas, 4)
                    important estuarine areas, 5) areas with concentrated coral reefs, areas with concentrated seagrass beds, 6)
                    natural shorelines in the coastal zone, 7) priority areas for biodiversity conservation, scenic spots, other
                    wetlands, etc. These areas have been evaluated to have significant ecological functions, extremely sensitive
                    and fragile ecological environments, or potential important ecological values. Any human activities within the
                    ERLs in Hainan are subject to the catalogue-based access management system. To this end, the Hainan
                    Provincial Government issued the Notice on the Revised Catalogue of Access Management for ERLs in Hainan
                    Province in 2023. The Notice is supported by 1) the access catalogue for the core zones of natural protected
                    areas in the ERLs; 2) the access catalogue for other zones within the ERLs. A project with activities that are
                    triggering the ERL, and a special justification report on "Limited Human Activities within the ERL" must be
                    prepared. DNRP/NRPBs will organize experts for technical review of the report before decision-making and
                    submit the case to the Hainan Provincial Government for approval.
 Mechanism of       In accordance with the Guiding Opinions on Establishing a System of Nature Protect Areas with National Parks
 natural            as the Main Body, China is accelerating the establishment of a nature protected areas system with national
 protected          parks as the main body and is earnestly strengthening the protection of natural ecology. To promote functional
 areas              optimization and system reorganization, a comprehensive evaluation has been conducted on all existing nature




                                                               33
                             reserves10 based on their natural attributes, ecological value, and management goals. This evaluation was
                             used to categorize them, gradually forming a classified system for nature protected areas that features national
                             parks as the main body, nature reserves as the foundation, and various types of natural parks as supplements.
                             In national parks and nature reserves, the protected areas are divided into core protected zones and general
                             control zones. In the core protected areas, human activities are generally prohibited; In the general control
                             areas, human activities are restricted. Nature parks are generally managed as general control zones. In
                             principle, development and production-related construction activities are prohibited in the general control zone.
                             However, some limited human activities that do not damage the ecological functions are allowed, such as
                             ecological monitoring, scientific research, and construction of necessary public facilities.
                             Natural protected areas are managed by FBs.
                             If the Project activities trigger any natural protected areas, the activities are subject to FBs review. If the review
                             is passed, FBs will grant initial permission to the access of the activities, subject to the government final
                             approval. The higher the protection level, the higher the review or approval level, depending on the type of
                             protected areas (See Table 4-7).
  Mechanism of               The various areas within the administrative area are divided into environmental units, categorized as priority
  Dynamic eco-               protection units,11 key control units,12 and general control units13. Based on the environmental unit, combined
  environment                with the delineation of the ‘ERLs, environmental quality baselines, threshold for resources utilization’, from the

                             Hainan is determined to be ecological-oriented and developed. Starting from 2024, after optimization, a total

                             (accounting for 11.5% and 10.4% of the land area and near-shore area respectively), and 69 are general control
                             units (accounting for 35.7% and 53.3% of the land area and near-shore area respectively). The Hainan

and environmental quality and the sustainable development of regional economy and society.

        2．Water and Soil Conservation
 Classified                 In accordance with the ‘Law on Water and Soil Conservation’ and other relevant provisions, in mountainous
 management                 areas, hilly areas, sandstorms and other areas prone to water and soil erosion or in production and construction
                            projects that may cause water and soil erosion 14 as defined in the WSC plans approved by the people's
                            governments at or above the county level or the departments authorized by them, the PIUs of production and
                            construction projects shall go through the following procedures to complete WSC scheme preparation,
                            submission, and approval before the commencement of production and construction projects: (a) a project with
                            land acquisition or occupation over 5 ha or earthwork or stonework over 50,000 m3 is subject to preparation of
                            a WSC report; (b) a project with land acquisition or occupation below 5 ha but over 0.5 ha or earthwork or
                            stonework below 50,000 m3 but over 1,000 m3 is subject to preparation of a WSC form; and (c) a project with
                            land acquisition or occupation below 0.5 ha or earthwork or stonework below 1,000 m 3 is exempted from
                            preparation of WSC schemes, but the responsible entity or individual should take measures to prevent soil
                            erosion to meet relevant technical standards.
 Procedures to              Approval: For a project that is approved, ratified, or filed by the State Council or relevant departments of the
 be followed for            State Council, the WSC reports should be approved by the Ministry of Water Resources. For a project that is
 WSC                        approved, ratified, or filed by local governments at the county level or above and the relevant departments, the
                            WSC reports should be approved by the competent department of water administration of the people's
                            government at the same level. For projects in cross-administrative areas, the WSC reports should be approved
                            by the common water conservancy administrative department at a higher level.
                            WSC monitoring and supervision: For large and medium-sized production and construction projects that
                            may cause serious soil erosion, the PIU shall organize the monitoring of soil erosion caused by production and
                            construction activities, timely and quantitatively evaluate the effectiveness of control measures, and report the
                            monitoring result to BWRs. The supervision of WSC of production and construction projects shall be carried
                            out.
                            WSC acceptance check at completion: Before a production and construction project is put into operation,
                            the PIU shall, carry out an independent inspection and acceptance of WSC facilities, and disclose the results
                            to public and report to the BWRs who approved WSC plans.
                            Supervision and inspection: BWRs are responsible for strengthening the supervision of the whole process
                            of the WSC plans, fully utilizing satellite remote sensing, drones, big data, internet and supervision’ and other
                            means to supervise and inspect the implementation, monitoring, and supervision of the WSC and acceptance
                            of the WSC facilities. The problems found should be handled in accordance with the law. Random sampling of
                            inspection targets at the annual rate of at least 10 percent and random selection of inspectors shall be
                            implemented and the regulatory information shall be disclosed on time.



4.2.2.3 Institutional Organization and Performance
53. It is noticed by the WB task team in its due diligence that some activities to be supported by the
Project (particularly those under RA1) will trigger the ERLs designated for Hainan Province. Such
activities are dominated by ecosystem restoration, located in natural parks that are subject to general
control management. They are neither located in national parks nor natural reserves, and never
involve any land acquisition, restricted access impacting livelihood. Some individual activities may
involve certain scales of land use temporarily and earthwork operations during their implementation,
and corresponding management requirements for ecological elements such as water and soil
conservation will be imposed. Therefore, the Project will rely on the existing institutional framework
and, through the collaborative efforts of relevant government authorities to ensure that ecological
risks are effectively controlled and the Project implementation is carried out in a standardized manner.

54. As discussed in the previous sections, in terms of ecological conservation management, Hainan
Province is similar to the rest of the country. The main government authorities, based on the
administrative management responsibilities empowered by national and local laws and regulations
related to ecological conservation, implement mechanisms of ERLs, natural protected areas, and
eco-environment zoning control. They conduct corresponding reviews and approvals during the
preparatory stage of the activities, and carry out post-event supervision after the activities are
implemented
⚫   DNRP/NRPBS are responsible for the assessment and adjustment of ERLs, the delineation and
    boundaries marking, as well as the control of land use in the territorial space. They take the lead
    to organizing the justification of limited human activities allowed within the ERLs, collaborating
    with relevant authorities to strengthen the implementation of ERLs mechanism. They oversee
    planning and construction of projects, take the lead to identify any ecological damage issue by
    means of judging remote sensing images plus field inspections, and supervise corrective
    measures.
⚫   FBs are responsible for organizing the supervision, management and guidance of forestry and
    coastal windbreak forests, natural protected areas, and their ecological conservation and
    restoration.
⚫   DEE/EEBs are responsible for EIAs management and regulatory of various pollution prevention
    and control to ensure bottom line of environmental quality, promoting the implementation of eco-
    environment zoning control mechanisms, key polluters’ credit evaluation and other mechanisms,
    and strengthening differentiated management.
⚫   The local governments are responsible for daily supervision, establishing a two-level linked
    inspection mechanism at the town/township and village levels, and stopping illegal occupation
    behaviors once they are found.
⚫   DWR/WRBs: play significant regulatory role in soil and water conservation, which is an important
    part of ecological protection.
55. Regulatory on activates within the scope of ERLs：The Project focuses on the protection and
restoration of coastal zone ecosystems. Most of the ecosystem restoration activities under RA1 are
designed and to be carried out within the scope of ERLs, based on the importance of ecological
functions and the restoration needs. Some successful cases of restoration activities that have been
carried out in Hainan Province indicate that the existing ecological conservation management system


                                                                36
is significantly effective and risks are controllable with maximized positive effect of restoration. Their
effective regulatory work can be reflected as follows:
⚫   Strict preliminary justification and review：during the preparation, based on relevant plans
    or implementation schemes, in addition to the feasibility studies, EIAs, and soil and water
    conservation plans that are generally required for project to be carried out in normal
    areas/sectors, if the Project involves sensitive ecological areas such as triggering ERLs and
    natural protected areas, a series of related special justification and review work will be carried
    out (as shown in the table below) until it is finally confirmed that the activities in the proposed
    project compliance with the requirements of Catalogue of Access Management for ERLs in
    Hainan Province to ensure that the activities will not go beyond the environmental quality
    baseline and resource utilization thresholds, and will comply with relevant regulations such as
    the Wetland Protection Regulations of Hainan Province, and be in conformity with relevant plans.
⚫   Scientific technical guidance and reserves: relevant technical guidance, specifications,
    standards formulated by the national authorities and the local authorities of Hainan Province
    (i.e., Technical Guidelines for Marine Ecological Restoration (Trial Version), Manual for
    Mangrove Ecological Restoration in Hainan Province, Technical Specifications on Ecological
    Public Forests (GB/T18337.3-2011); Forest Planting Technical Specifications on Afforestation,
    Specifications on Forest Tending, "Technical Specifications on Degraded Forest Restoration
    (Trial Version), Quality Classification of Main Forest Planting Tree Species Seedlings" (GB6000-
    1999), Quality Classification of Forest Seeds (GB7908-1999) etc.) are in place. They specify
    the technical requirements on the principles, flowchart to be followed for marine and forest
    ecosystem restoration. They also specify such technical requirements in terms of problem
    diagnosis, basic requirements, restoring measures, monitoring and evaluation of restoring
    effects. These technical guidelines, specifications, and standards provided scientific technical
    guidance to ensure the activities are technically reliable, economically feasible. Hainan Province
    has carried out numerous research programs and accumulated a lot of experience in the
    establishment of coastal windbreak forests. For instance, “studies on the ecological restoration
    model and comprehensive benefits of coastal windbreak forests”, the “application of water-
    retaining agents in afforestation and forest protection in Hainan”, the “research on NbS renewal
    of Casuarina equisetifolia L. for transformation of low-efficiency coastal windbreak forest”, the
    “monitoring of biomass and carbon sequestration of Casuarina equisetifolia L in the eastern
    coastal areas, the “coastal zone ecological restoration and rehabilitation, and the “application of
    native tree species cultivation techniques”, etc. Furthermore, with the strong supports from
    universities and research institutions such as Hainan University, Hainan Normal University, and
    the Provincial Forestry Research Institute in fields afforestation technology, especially the
    presence of the Chinese Forestry Research Institute's academician workstation in Hainan, and
    the professional guidance from domestic and provincial universities and research units in
    afforestation, technical reserves and guarantees are obtained in Hainan.
⚫   Specified working procedures with M&E: A typical ecosystem restoration includes such
    working procedures as preliminary investigation → problem diagnosis → setting restoration
    goals → selection of restoration approaches → ascertaining restoration plans → implementation
    of ecological restoration → follow-up monitoring, effect evaluation and adaptive management.
    Restoration activities follow the principles of problem-oriented approach, adaptive to local
    conditions, NbS with human assistance efforts, systematic restoration for both marine and land
    in a reasonable and feasible manner with controllable risks. For example: In the restoration
    projects that have been carried out in Changjiang and Lingshui mentioned earlier, the relevant
    data provided to the WB task team show that: During the initial stage of these projects, the
    necessary surveys were conduct by professionals, (including baseline of marine ecological
    environment, land-sea engineering survey, hydrology, hydrodynamics, water environment
    investigations and monitoring, numerical simulation studies of tidal currents, sediment and
    waves, etc.). Starting from problem diagnosis, setting restoration goals, methods, plans, till
    contract signature for implementation of the restoration, as well as the three-year management
    period (unlike the civil works contract which includes 1 year defects liability period), acceptance
    and follow-up monitoring and evaluation, all of them were carried out in accordance with relevant
    guidelines, procedures and standards. Take another project on mangrove restoration project
    carried out within the scope of an ERL in Lingshui County as example, in order to remove

                                                    37
                                   laguncularia racemose, an invasive species encroaching on the ecological niche of the
                                   mangroves, both mechanical and manual removal methods were used, the root systems were
                                   cleared to prevent the regrowth of laguncularia racemose. At the same time, a zone-based
                                   operation approach was adopted to maximize the protection of original native mangroves,
                                   avoiding irreversible damage to the stability and resilience of the entire mangrove ecosystem.
                                   Part of the trucks of the removed laguncularia racemose were used to build the cofferdam, rest
                                   were hauled away from the mangrove wetland for multi-purpose utilization and avoiding
                                   secondary pollution. For the enrichment planting process, native mangrove tree species that
                                   are suitable for local conditions are selected. Mechanism of "license-certificates-label" was
                                   implemented to ensure the healthy seedlings without pests and quarantine objects are delivered
                                   to the Project site. After replantation, regular monitoring and three-year
                                   management/maintenance period were carried out to ensure plants survival rate,
                                   phytocoenosium density until birds return. These good practices have served as a model for
                                   managing the potential adverse impacts and risks on the environment that may arise from the
                                   activities within the scope of ERLs to be supported by the Project.
